Authentic and Delicious!
Sunday night at 630 and the Fuji Sukiyaki was busy. We were greeted by efficient wait staff who let us know we would have a 20 min wait. We were seated 20 min later but had to wait another 15 min before we were served. Once our order was taken we were treated to delicious Miso soup then we selected an assortment of rolls and sashimi. Everything was fresh, delicious, and perfectly prepared. The prices were excellent for the area and we decided we will be back soon and often.</review>

< review>
Walked in on a Saturday afternoon to no wait. Surprised to see how small the place is inside (although they do have a back area for large parties). Service was lackluster and food okay.

The photos on Yelp made the sushi look so appetizing, but the rolls were nothing to rave about. They were small and not well made.

I would stick to the nigiri and sashimi here as it seems to be their specialty. The oyster bomb and sunrise nigiri were pretty good.

Overall it was a decent place for some variety of nigiri, but nothing too special.< /review>

<time>1384889058868<//time><Rating>4</Rating>< Text>
Had a last minute change of plans for lunch due to our original planned lunch spot being closed, so I pulled out my handy dandy yelp mobile app to come to the rescue and found Fuji Sukiyaki.  I was a little nervous coming in due to some mixed reviews, but figured that it as worth a shot.

I was very pleasantly surprised by this sushi spot.  The fish was very fresh, the rolls were delicious and the sashimi was amazing.  I highly recommend the Tuna Poki if you are looking for sashimi with a little more flavor to it.

The only negative was the service - we were one of 4 groups in the entire restaurant, so I was disappointed by how long it took to take our order or get us the check when we were clearly done with our meal.

Aside from that, it was a great meal!<//Text>

< review>
Feels like a small town "mom & pop" shop, from Japan. Never been there, but it feels like a midwestern diner - just not serving midwestern food. I've eaten here several times and not been left down.

Food: Good. I only have their vegan-friendly sushi, but dine here with friends. I've never seen anyone be sad about their sushi. It's consistenly done well and not trying to be fancy.

Staff: Prompt, courteous, not warm per-se, but friendly enough to get the order taken and food delivered.

Atmosphere: LIke I said, mom & pop diner. They also have some traditional seating with rice paper doors. I've never had the pleasure, but it's quaint and does not feel forced.

Always happy to eat here. I don't rave about it to my friends, but it's kinda my mental standard for sushi.<//review>

< review>
2.5 - For a place with sukiyaki in its name, it sure had a distracted menu with sukiyaki buried in a corner. Got the beef sukiyaki for $9.95, but this was the first time it came pre-cooked in a metal bowl, so not really a real sukiyaki experience. Flavors were alright, a bit stingy on the beef, but it came with tofu, cabbage, Shitake mushrooms, and vermicelli. It was almost like eating a nabeyaki udon, except with beef and vermicelli instead of chicken and udon. Came with a bowl of rice and miso soup.

Bento box of tempura and chicken katsu for $7.95, but the batter was thick and not particularly good. Came with miso soup.

Came with Chinese pickled cabbage.

Not busy during lunch, but waitress wasn't attentive. I'm fairly certain this place is Chinese-run. Takes credit. On the outskirt of San Mateo downtown, but I recommend heading into the center for authentic Japanese food.< /review>

<UserId.>106729804623790685738<//UserId.>< user_name>
condor< /user_name>
<date>1592164656930</date><rating>1<//rating>< text>
My Husband and I moved from Idaho in Feb to California. We researched a good storage option, and decided on North Main Street Storage and booked a package through THEIR website. Well when we got there from our 2 day drive from Idaho with all of our things, we show up to the storage unit only to be harassed by the manager (Diana, her name is everywhere. I couldn't forget it if I tried) telling us that the special we had email proof that we received "doesn't exist" and she tried to bully us into paying the full $190 a month for the unit-- which I of course refused and told her she would honor the $80 deal we received. She agreed to do that for 4 months and would put notes into the system so we didn't get charged the full amount. So we moved into our unit.

The following month I called in 4 days before rent was due to pay-- she couldn't find her notes and was insisting I needed to pay the $190 rent. I refused and told her to keep looking. Diana eventually remembered our interaction the month prior so she allowed us to pay the prorated rent and assured me that she would make sure to have notes on our account this time. Then 2 weeks later while in Texas visiting family I get a call from my mother telling me that we got a letter from our storage place and asked if she should open it, I agreed. The letter was a threat for not "paying full rent" telling us they were going to lock us out of our unit if it wasn't paid within a few days. I was livid and called North Main Storage only to get Diana. She tried to convince me I was wrong AGAIN. Then after 20 mins on the phone "found her notes" and assured me we wouldn't be kicked out of our unit.

< Text>
When I googled for the closest L&L Hawaiian BBQ nearby, this popped up as the closest. This isn't even an L&L chain (trying to tell google about it atm)? I called and had a hard time placing my order with the woman (she didn't speak proper english) that picked up the phone. I did the take out option. I ordered the BBQ mix plate and BBQ chicken plate.

Their food tastes similar to L&L but I would prefer L&L for the following reasons...
1. More quantity for your money (They provide more vegetables and rice on the side at L&L) than this plc.
2. This plc charges $1.50 to change the macaroni side to vegetables.

This plc also sells doughnuts on the side. So when you walk in, it has a little funky set up.</Text>

< Review>
9/28/2020
Approximately 18 months ago, my husband canceled our service plan for which we were paying a monthly fee. Around that time, the company stopped their courtesy reminders to schedule maintenance. However, they did NOT inform us of this change in practice. Our bank continued to issue auto-payments to the company. When I performed an audit I found that the company continued to cash our checks despite not delivering any services.

I called mid-July and left a message with customer service but didn't hear back until they noticed I had stopped payments. Then I had their attention. *Three weeks later* (in early August)I received a call back. The service agent I spoke with said that she could put me back on the courtesy reminder call list. Mind you, I was *never informed* that I was removed from the list in the first place! Also we had already cancelled services. Conveniently, she could not find any documentation of the cancellation. During all my interactions I have not been able to get an email address when I call the company number.

They put the responsibility for asking for services back on the consumer after selling us a "discounted" maintenance plan. Then, the company could not find any documentation of our cancellation, so in order to obtain a refund, the service agent said she would have to forward the request to her supervisor. Approximately 6 weeks later, I have not heard back from the agent. But guess what? I received another bill even after I was assured that my account was closed.

So I call back yet again and speak to another agent who sees all the notes in my account confirming my account of the events. She cancels the most recent bill, but I have yet to hear back from the company regarding the prior payments accepted without services rendered. You would think that if a customer had not received services for more than 18 months, they would at least call to check in, rather than just continue to cash the checks.

I recognize the shared responsibility on our end. I am hoping the company will do the right thing and issue a refund for the service fees collected after services ceased.

I will update this review as events proceed.

Update 10/1/20:
I received a call from the accounting department to let me know that they agreed to a partial refund of the checks that they cashed. I will receive approximately 2/3 of the funds mistakenly paid to the company.
This resolution is satisfactory. I am increasing my rating of this company from 1 to 3 stars.< /Review>

The technician was great tested the water, showed me I wasn't rinsing enough, and assured me all was well with my system. I bought the under the sink water purification system as well as the soft water one. It's nice to be able to drink great tasting water right from the tap, and I'm saving a bundle on soap, and detergent as well. An added benefit is that I've haven't had any more stops up in the kitchen sink as the soft water actually stops build up in the pipes, and even takes out the deposits already in them over time. This was one of my main reasons for buying the system, as I don't want to have to re-pipe my 25 year old home.
